  {state next : Hibana.CommitState} {eventId : Nat},
  @Eq.{1} Bool certificate.check true →
    @Eq.{1} Hibana.AdmissionResult
        (Hibana.descriptorCursorStep certificate.image (Hibana.projectGraph certificate.image.role certificate.choreo)
          state eventId)
        (Hibana.AdmissionResult.accepted next) →
      And
        (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} (List.{0} Hibana.LocalAction)) certificate.image.decodeActions?
          (@some.{0} (List.{0} Hibana.LocalAction)
            (@List.map.{0, 0} Hibana.Event Hibana.LocalAction Hibana.Event.action
              (Hibana.projectGraph certificate.image.role certificate.choreo).events)))
        (@Exists.{1} Hibana.DescriptorOperation fun operation =>
          @Exists.{1} Hibana.Event fun event =>
            And
              (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Hibana.DescriptorOperation) (certificate.image.eventOperation? eventId)
                (@some.{0} Hibana.DescriptorOperation operation))
              (And (@Eq.{1} Nat operation.eventId eventId)
                (And (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Nat) (certificate.image.eventLane? eventId) (@some.{0} Nat operation.lane))
                  (And
                    (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Nat) (certificate.image.eventFrameLabel? eventId)
                      (@some.{0} Nat operation.frameLabel))
                    (And
                      (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Hibana.Event)
                        (@getElem?.{0, 0, 0} (List.{0} Hibana.Event) Nat Hibana.Event
                          (fun as i => @LT.lt.{0} Nat instLTNat i (@List.length.{0} Hibana.Event as))
                          (@List.instGetElem?NatLtLength.{0} Hibana.Event)

                        (@some.{0} Hibana.Event event))
                      (And (@Eq.{1} Nat event.id eventId)

                          (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Hibana.CommitState)

                              eventId)

@Hibana.accepted_descriptor_pipelined_send_extends_elastic_history : ∀ {descriptor : Hibana.ExactDescriptorCertificate}
  {cursor nextCursor : Hibana.CommitState} {event : Hibana.GlobalEvent} {history : Hibana.ElasticAdmissionHistory}
  {globalId peer label schema : Nat},
  @Eq.{1} Bool descriptor.check true →
    @Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent)
        (@getElem?.{0, 0, 0} (List.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent) Nat Hibana.GlobalEvent
          (fun as i => @LT.lt.{0} Nat instLTNat i (@List.length.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent as))
          (@List.instGetElem?NatLtLength.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent) descriptor.choreo.globalEvents globalId)
        (@some.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent event) →
      @Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Hibana.LocalAction) (event.action? descriptor.image.role)
          (@some.{0} Hibana.LocalAction (Hibana.LocalAction.send peer label schema)) →
        history.MatchesEventChannel event →
          history.WellFormed →
            @Eq.{1} Hibana.AdmissionResult
                (Hibana.descriptorCursorStep descriptor.image
                  (Hibana.projectGraph descriptor.image.role descriptor.choreo) cursor
                  (Hibana.Choreo.localEventId descriptor.image.role globalId descriptor.choreo))
                (Hibana.AdmissionResult.accepted nextCursor) →
              have eventId := Hibana.Choreo.localEventId descriptor.image.role globalId descriptor.choreo;
              have key := history.nextOccurrence globalId;
              have nextHistory := history.appendOccurrence globalId;
              And
                (@Eq.{1} (Option.{0} Hibana.LocalAction) (descriptor.image.eventAction? eventId)
                  (@some.{0} Hibana.LocalAction (Hibana.LocalAction.send peer label schema)))
                (And nextHistory.WellFormed
                  (And (@Eq.{1} Hibana.TransportChannel nextHistory.channel history.channel)
                    (And
                      (@Eq.{1} (List.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey) nextHistory.accepted
                        (@HAppend.hAppend.{0, 0, 0} (List.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey)
                          (List.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey) (List.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey)
                          (@instHAppendOfAppend.{0} (List.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey)
                            (@List.instAppend.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey))
                          history.accepted
                          (@List.cons.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey key (@List.nil.{0} Hibana.ElasticOccurrenceKey))))
                      (And (@Eq.{1} Nat key.iteration (history.nextIteration globalId))
                        (nextHistory.MatchesEventChannel event)))))

          config.CancellationWellFormed →

              And (Hibana.CancellationReachable config retired)

                      @Eq.{1} Hibana.GlobalSessionStatus retired.status (Hibana.GlobalSessionStatus.retired cause))

@Hibana.verified_protocol_roll_reentry_has_fifo_or_causal_order : ∀ {certificate : Hibana.VerifiedProtocolCertificate}
  {session roleCount : Nat} {choreo body : Hibana.Choreo},
  @Eq.{1} Bool (certificate.check session roleCount choreo) true →
    @Membership.mem.{0, 0} Hibana.Choreo (List.{0} Hibana.Choreo) (@List.instMembership.{0} Hibana.Choreo)
        choreo.rollBodies body →
      ∀ {left right : Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence},
        @Membership.mem.{0, 0} Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence (List.{0} Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence)
            (@List.instMembership.{0} Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence) body.staticGlobalOccurrences left →
          @Membership.mem.{0, 0} Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence (List.{0} Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence)
              (@List.instMembership.{0} Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence) body.staticGlobalOccurrences right →
            @Ne.{1} Nat left.event.sender left.event.receiver →
              @Ne.{1} Nat right.event.sender right.event.receiver →
                @Eq.{1} Nat left.event.receiver right.event.receiver →
                  @Eq.{1} Nat left.event.lane right.event.lane →
                    @LT.lt.{0} Nat instLTNat right.event.receiver roleCount →
                      Or (@Eq.{1} Nat left.event.sender right.event.sender)
                        (Hibana.CausalHandoffPath body.rollUnfoldedOccurrences
                          (Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence.inRollIteration
                            (@List.length.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent body.globalEvents) Hibana.StaticRollIteration.current
                            left)
                          (Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence.inRollIteration
                            (@List.length.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent body.globalEvents) Hibana.StaticRollIteration.next
                            right)
                          roleCount
                          (Hibana.StaticGlobalOccurrence.inRollIteration
                            (@List.length.{0} Hibana.GlobalEvent body.globalEvents) Hibana.StaticRollIteration.next
                            right))
